from ForestDiffusion import ForestDiffusionModel ^XIYEvh4L

# Iris: numpy dataset with 4 variables (all numerical) and 1 outcome (categorical) ^aAW0IVNK

from sklearn.datasets import load_iris ^j6W1ERLH

import numpy as np ^otTdwPt8

my_data = load_iris() ^CHfmZXpa

X, y = my_data['data'], my_data['target'] ^a48wicy4

Xy = np.concatenate((X, np.expand_dims(y, axis=1)), axis=1) ^iVGNUDyW

# Classification problem (outcome is categorical) ^HsDZC52c

forest_model = ForestDiffusionModel(X, label_y=y, n_t=50, duplicate_K=100, bin_indexes=[], cat_indexes=[], int_indexes=[], diffusion_type='flow', n_jobs=-1) ^lLhemtxT

Xy_fake = forest_model.generate(batch_size=X.shape[0]) # last variable will be the label_y ^LsS37vyO

# Regression problem (outcome is continuous) ^wJT8kkJU

Xy = np.concatenate((X, np.expand_dims(y, axis=1)), axis=1) ^g1Hysb0A

forest_model = ForestDiffusionModel(Xy, n_t=50, duplicate_K=100, bin_indexes=[], cat_indexes=[4], int_indexes=[], diffusion_type='flow', n_jobs=-1) ^2z1ulCeI

Xy_fake = forest_model.generate(batch_size=X.shape[0]) ^0TMmCZCS

Autoencoder converts it into a tensor ^cJz10JTl

X = numpy array of features
y =numpy array of target ^VKElUx3T

Dataframne(minority)
 ^n73oKXbB

Tensor ^kgTCf92M

  ^BHKFTnGV

y =numpy array of target ^68HwoUT2
